""SELECT [a].[AMST_Id], [a].[AMST_FirstName], [a].[AMST_MiddleName], [a].[AMST_LastName], LTRIM(RTRIM((((CASE
    WHEN [a].[AMST_FirstName] IS NULL
    THEN N' ' ELSE [a].[AMST_FirstName]
END + N' ') + CASE
    WHEN [a].[AMST_MiddleName] IS NULL
    THEN N' ' ELSE [a].[AMST_MiddleName]
END) + N' ') + CASE
    WHEN [a].[AMST_LastName] IS NULL
    THEN N' ' ELSE [a].[AMST_LastName]
END)) AS [amst_FirstName0], LTRIM(RTRIM((CASE
    WHEN [a].[AMST_FirstName] IS NULL OR ([a].[AMST_FirstName] = N'')
    THEN N'' ELSE N' ' + [a].[AMST_FirstName]
END + CASE
    WHEN ([a].[AMST_MiddleName] IS NULL OR ([a].[AMST_MiddleName] = N'')) OR ([a].[AMST_MiddleName] = N'0')
